    75:       if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") {
    76:         window.localStorage.removeItem(key);
    77:       } else {
    78:         window.localStorage.setItem(key, String(value));
    79:       }
    80:     } catch (error) {
    81:       /* storage unavailable */
    82:     }
    83:   }

  1087: function aicmAxcFindElement(ids) {
  1088:   for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i += 1) {
  1089:     var el = document.getElementById(ids[i]);
  1090:     if (el) return el;
  1091:   }
  1092:   return null;

  1094: 
  1095: function aicmAxcCatalogRowByValue(value) {
  1096:   var text = String(value || "").trim();
  1097:   if (!text) return null;
  1098:   var rows = typeof aicmRobotCatalogSafe === "function" ? aicmRobotCatalogSafe() : [];
  1099:   for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i += 1) {
  1100:     var row = rows[i] || {};
  1101:     var values = [
  1102:       typeof aicmRobotValue === "function" ? aicmRobotValue(row) : "",
  1103:       row.robot_pool_id,
  1104:       row.business_robot_pool_id,
  1105:       row.aicm_robot_pool_id,
  1106:       row.worker_pool_id,
  1107:       row.placement_robot_pool_id,
  1108:       row.aiworker_model_code,
  1109:       row.model_code,
  1110:       row.robot_id
  1111:     ].map(function (item) { return String(item || "").trim(); });
  1112: 
  1113:     if (values.indexOf(text) >= 0) return row;
  1114:   }
  1115:   return null;

  1789: function aicmRobotRoleText(row) {

  2087: function aicmAxnNormalizeRole(roleCode) {

  2866: function renderTree(departments) {
  2867:     if (departments.length === 0) {
  2868:       return [
  2869:         '<div class="aicm-empty-state">',
  2870:         '  <strong>部門がまだありません</strong>',
  2871:         '  <p>選択中のAI企業に部門を追加すると、ここに階層表示されます。</p>',
  2872:         '  <div class="aicm-dashboard-action-row">',
  2873:         '    <button type="button" data-core-action="go" data-screen="department-new">部門新規追加</button>',
  2874:         '  </div>',
  2875:         '</div>'
  2876:       ].join("");
  2877:     }
  2878: 
  2879:     return [
  2880:       '<div class="aicm-tree-toolbar">',
  2881:       '  <button type="button" data-core-action="go" data-screen="department-new">部門新規追加</button>',
  2882:       '  <button type="button" data-core-action="go" data-screen="section-new">課新規追加</button>',
  2883:       '</div>',
  2884:       '<div class="aicm-org-tree">',
  2885:       departments.map(function (department) {
  2886:         var sections = departmentSections(department.aicm_user_company_department_id);

    65:   function readStorage(key) {
    66:     try {
    67:       return window.localStorage.getItem(key) || "";
    68:     } catch (error) {
    69:       return "";
    70:     }
    71:   }
    72: 
    73:   function writeStorage(key, value) {
    74:     try {
    75:       if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") {
    76:         window.localStorage.removeItem(key);
    77:       } else {
    78:         window.localStorage.setItem(key, String(value));
    79:       }
    80:     } catch (error) {
    81:       /* storage unavailable */
    82:     }
    83:   }
    84: 
    85:   function list(value) {
    86:     return Array.isArray(value) ? value : [];
    87:   }
    88: 
    89:   function text(value) {
    90:     return value === null || value === undefined ? "" : String(value);
    91:   }

    94:     return text(value)

   565:   function renderMessages() {
   566:     var parts = [];
   567: 
   568:     if (state.loading) {
   569:       parts.push('<div class="aicm-core-message">読込中...</div>');
   570:     }
   571: 
   572:     if (state.noticeMessage) {
   573:       parts.push('<div class="aicm-core-message aicm-core-message-ok">' + escapeHtml(state.noticeMessage) + '</div>');
   574:     }
   575: 
   576:     if (state.errorMessage) {
   577:       parts.push('<div class="aicm-core-message aicm-core-message-error">' + escapeHtml(state.errorMessage) + '</div>');
   578:     }
   579: 
   580:     return parts.join("");
   581:   }

  1095: function aicmAxcCatalogRowByValue(value) {
  1096:   var text = String(value || "").trim();
  1097:   if (!text) return null;
  1098:   var rows = typeof aicmRobotCatalogSafe === "function" ? aicmRobotCatalogSafe() : [];
  1099:   for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i += 1) {
  1100:     var row = rows[i] || {};
  1101:     var values = [
  1102:       typeof aicmRobotValue === "function" ? aicmRobotValue(row) : "",
  1103:       row.robot_pool_id,
  1104:       row.business_robot_pool_id,
  1105:       row.aicm_robot_pool_id,
  1106:       row.worker_pool_id,
  1107:       row.placement_robot_pool_id,
  1108:       row.aiworker_model_code,
  1109:       row.model_code,
  1110:       row.robot_id
  1111:     ].map(function (item) { return String(item || "").trim(); });
  1112: 
  1113:     if (values.indexOf(text) >= 0) return row;
  1114:   }
  1115:   return null;
  1116: }

  1118: function aicmAxcSelectedRobotMeta(selectOrId) {
  1119:   var el = typeof selectOrId === "string" ? document.getElementById(selectOrId) : selectOrId;
  1120:   if (!el) return null;
  1121: 
  1122:   var selectedValue = String(el.value || "").trim();
  1123:   var opt = el.options && el.selectedIndex >= 0 ? el.options[el.selectedIndex] : null;
  1124:   var row = aicmAxcCatalogRowByValue(selectedValue) || {};
  1125: 
  1126:   var robotPoolId = String(
  1127:     row.robot_pool_id ||
  1128:     row.business_robot_pool_id ||
  1129:     row.aicm_robot_pool_id ||
  1130:     row.worker_pool_id ||
  1131:     row.placement_robot_pool_id ||
  1132:     (aicmAxcUuidLike(selectedValue) ? selectedValue : "")
  1133:   ).trim();
  1134: 
  1135:   var modelCode = String(
  1136:     row.aiworker_model_code ||
  1137:     row.model_code ||
  1138:     row.aiworkerModelCode ||

  1140:     (!aicmAxcUuidLike(selectedValue) ? selectedValue : "")
  1141:   ).trim();
  1142: 
  1143:   if (!robotPoolId && !modelCode) return null;
  1144:

    65:   function readStorage(key) {
    66:     try {
    67:       return window.localStorage.getItem(key) || "";
    68:     } catch (error) {
    69:       return "";
    70:     }
    71:   }

    73:   function writeStorage(key, value) {
    74:     try {
    75:       if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") {
    76:         window.localStorage.removeItem(key);
    77:       } else {
    78:         window.localStorage.setItem(key, String(value));
    79:       }
    80:     } catch (error) {
    81:       /* storage unavailable */
    82:     }
    83:   }

  1681: function aicmRoleScopeMatches(row, scope) {
  1682:     if (!row || !scope) return false;
  1683: 
  1684:     if (scope.companyId && row.aicm_user_company_id && row.aicm_user_company_id !== scope.companyId) return false;
  1685: 
  1686:     if (scope.departmentId) {
  1687:       var rowDepartmentId = row.aicm_user_company_department_id || row.department_id || "";
  1688:       if (rowDepartmentId && rowDepartmentId !== scope.departmentId) return false;
  1689:     }
  1690: 
  1691:     if (scope.sectionId) {
  1692:       var rowSectionId = row.aicm_user_company_section_id || row.section_id || "";
  1693:       if (rowSectionId && rowSectionId !== scope.sectionId) return false;
  1694:     }
  1695: 
  1696:     return true;
  1697:   }

  1699: function aicmCurrentRolePlacements(roleCode, scope) {
  1700:     var ctx = typeof aicmCtxSafe === "function" ? aicmCtxSafe() : (state.context || state || {});
  1701:     var placements = Array.isArray(ctx.placements) ? ctx.placements : [];
  1702: 
  1703:     return placements.filter(function (row) {
  1704:       return aicmPlacementMatchesRole(row, roleCode) && aicmRoleScopeMatches(row, scope);
  1705:     });

  3738: function downloadTextFile(filename, text, mimeType) {
  3739:     var blob = new Blob([String(text || "")], { type: mimeType || "text/plain;charset=utf-8" });
  3740:     var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  3741:     var a = document.createElement("a");
  3742:     a.href = url;
  3743:     a.download = filename;
  3744:     document.body.appendChild(a);
  3745:     a.click();
  3746:     a.remove();
  3747:     setTimeout(function () {
  3748:       URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  3749:     }, 1000);
  3750:   }
  3751: 
  3752:   async function readTaskLedgerCsvFile(file) {
  3753:     if (!file) return;
  3754: 
  3755:     try {
  3756:       var text = await file.text();
  3757:       state.csvImportText = text;
  3758:       state.csvImportFileName = file.name || "selected.csv";
  3759:       state.csvImportPreview = [];
  3760:       state.csvImportLastResult = "";
  3761:       setMessage("ok", "CSVファイルを読み込みました: " + state.csvImportFileName);
  3762:     } catch (error) {
  3763:       state.csvImportText = "";
